#include <stdio.h>

int main() {
  int i = 0;
  int limit = 100; // Assuming a limit value of 100 for illustration purposes
  char str[limit];

  while (i < limit - 1 && (c = getchar()) != EOF) {

  printf("%s\n", str); // Print the captured input string
}

                '{ option_block_item_list }'

Received response: {
  // Check if the string starts with '{'
  if (str[0] != '{') {
    printf("Syntax Error: Missing '{' at the beginning.\n");
    return;
  }

  int i = 1;
  int count = 1;

  // Parse through the string to check the syntax
  while (str[i] != '\0') {
    if (str[i] == '{') {
      count++;
    } else if (str[i] == '}') {
      count--;
      if (count == 0) {
        printf("Syntax Correct: Properly balanced '{}'.\n");
        return;
      }
    }
    i++;
  }

  // If count is not zero, then there are unmatched curly braces
  if (count != 0) {
    printf("Syntax Error: Unmatched curly braces.\n");
  }
}

      brackets++;
    }
    else if (str[i] == ']')
    {
      brackets--;
    }
    else if (str[i] == '{')
    {
      braces++;
    }
    else if (str[i] == '}')
    {
      braces--;
    }
    else if (str[i] == '\'')
    {
      single_quotes++;
    }
    else if (str[i] == '\"')
    {
      double_quotes++;
    }
    else if (str[i] == '/' && str[i + 1] == '/')
    {
      comments++;
      break;
    }

    i++;
  }

  if (parentheses == 0 && brackets == 0 && braces == 0 && single_quotes % 2 == 0 && double_quotes % 2 == 0 && comments == 0)
  {
    printf("Syntax is correct.\n");
  }
  else
  {
    printf("Syntax is incorrect.\n");
  }
}

        ++braces;
      }
      else if (str[i] == '}')

        --braces;
      }
